<p>Source data of the figures are provided with this paper. All datasets in this paper have been deposited in the NASA Open Science Data Repositories (OSDR; osdr.nasa.gov; comprised of GeneLab<sup><a href="#CR92" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR92">92</a></sup> and the Ames Life Sciences Data Archive [ALSDA]<sup><a href="#CR1" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR1">1</a>,<a href="#CR99" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR99">99</a></sup>). Identifiers for publicly downloadable datasets in the OSDR are documented below. Also, data can be visualized online through the SOMA Data Explorer (link below) with the latest reference<sup><a href="#CR100" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR100">100</a></sup>. Any additional information required to reanalyze the data reported in this work is available from the Lead Contact upon request. For the blood plasma, the following assays are found under OSDR identifier OSD-571: Proteomics (Seer Proteograph), proteomics of blood EVPs, plasma metabolomics data, cell-free RNA. Direct RNA-seq from blood plasma can be found under OSDR identifier: OSD-569 (Supplementary Table <a href="#MOESM1" class="usa-link">1</a>) All raw data, processed data and detailed methods are in the GeneLab OSDR links here: <a href="https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-569" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-569</a><a href="https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-571" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-571</a> Interactive data browser for the proteomics, metabolomics, and other omics data are available on the SOMA data portal: <a href="https://soma.weill.cornell.edu/apps/SOMA_Browser/" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://soma.weill.cornell.edu/apps/SOMA_Browser/</a> <a href="#Sec30" class="usa-link">Source data</a> are provided with this paper.</p></section><section id="notes4"><h2 class="pmc_sec_title">Code availability</h2>

<p class="font-secondary"><em>This section collects any data citations, data availability statements, or supplementary materials included in this article.</em></p>

<section class="sm xbox font-sm" id="db_ds_supplementary-material1_reqid_"><div class="media p"><div class="caption">
<a href="/articles/instance/11166969/bin/41467_2024_48841_MOESM1_ESM.pdf" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" class="usa-link">Supplementary Information</a><sup> (1.6MB, pdf) </sup>

<a href="/articles/instance/11166969/bin/41467_2024_48841_MOESM3_ESM.pdf" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" class="usa-link">Reporting Summary</a><sup> (74.5KB, pdf) </sup>
</div></div></section><section class="sm xbox font-sm" id="db_ds_supplementary-material4_reqid_"><div class="media p"><div class="caption">
<a href="/articles/instance/11166969/bin/41467_2024_48841_MOESM4_ESM.zip" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" class="usa-link">Source Data</a><sup> (3MB, zip) </sup>
</div></div></section></section><section id="_adda93_" lang="en" class="data-availability-statement"><h3 class="pmc_sec_title">Data Availability Statement</h3>
<p>Source data of the figures are provided with this paper. All datasets in this paper have been deposited in the NASA Open Science Data Repositories (OSDR; osdr.nasa.gov; comprised of GeneLab<sup><a href="#CR92" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR92">92</a></sup> and the Ames Life Sciences Data Archive [ALSDA]<sup><a href="#CR1" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR1">1</a>,<a href="#CR99" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR99">99</a></sup>). Identifiers for publicly downloadable datasets in the OSDR are documented below. Also, data can be visualized online through the SOMA Data Explorer (link below) with the latest reference<sup><a href="#CR100" class="usa-link" aria-describedby="CR100">100</a></sup>. Any additional information required to reanalyze the data reported in this work is available from the Lead Contact upon request. For the blood plasma, the following assays are found under OSDR identifier OSD-571: Proteomics (Seer Proteograph), proteomics of blood EVPs, plasma metabolomics data, cell-free RNA. Direct RNA-seq from blood plasma can be found under OSDR identifier: OSD-569 (Supplementary Table <a href="#MOESM1" class="usa-link">1</a>) All raw data, processed data and detailed methods are in the GeneLab OSDR links here: <a href="https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-569" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-569</a><a href="https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-571" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://osdr.nasa.gov/bio/repo/data/studies/OSD-571</a> Interactive data browser for the proteomics, metabolomics, and other omics data are available on the SOMA data portal: <a href="https://soma.weill.cornell.edu/apps/SOMA_Browser/" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://soma.weill.cornell.edu/apps/SOMA_Browser/</a> <a href="#Sec30" class="usa-link">Source data</a> are provided with this paper.</p>
<p>All code used to generate the analyses in this manuscript are available on GitHub at <a href="https://github.com/eliah-o/inspiration4-omics" class="usa-link usa-link--external" data-ga-action="click_feat_suppl" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">https://github.com/eliah-o/inspiration4-omics</a>.</p></section></section></section><footer class="p courtesy-note font-secondary font-sm text-center"><hr class="headless">
<p>Articles from Nature Communications are provided here courtesy of <strong>Nature Publishing Group</strong></p></footer></section></article>
